Hardware. Price of classic products = boutique < treasure < premium. I have been staying for a long time and have seen it in person with pictures. Jiangxiang Technology is indeed a state-owned enterprise. The basic area of ‚Äã‚Äãthe medium-sized room type is too small according to the current 5-star standard! As for the premium, the basic room is almost the top in Sanya. It is the result of the guidance of state-owned enterprise-level thinking. With an area of ‚Äã‚Äãmore than 300 acres, more than 700 rooms, a large number of public areas and green spaces, if the leaders live in the premium, the lower-level rooms can only actively lower the standards. It is a pity that the treasure should be configured according to the standard 5-star, but the basic room is not equipped with a bathtub, and it is basically impossible to upgrade in the later stage. 2. Service. When checking in, Chen Jiaodan, the housekeeper, took the initiative to add WeChat. It seems that all hotels in Sanya are like this now. It is also good and can solve the problem of the hotel interval in time. All questions were answered, without excessively proactive recommendations or asking for good reviews. On the day of check-in, the luggage was sent to the room. On the last day, the flight was late, and the check-out was delayed to 3 pm. The receptionists at the door were all young guys, and there were electric cars to shuttle between 4 different hotels. 3. Swimming pool. There is a rare indoor heated swimming pool in Sanya, and the outdoor swimming pool is in front of the luxury hotel. 4. Breakfast. It was quite satisfactory. This time I came to Hainan for 6 days and found that the three hotels I stayed in, Marriott, Holiday Inn, and Moutai, all reduced meat dishes. There was basically no meat in the Marriott in Xiangshui Bay, and there was a smoked salmon in Moutai Treasure. When the meal was collected at 10 o'clock, the remaining food was indeed poured out in front of the review. I guess it was to let everyone see that it was fresh every day, and the rest was dealt with in time. Anyway, Moutai is not short of money. 5. Treasure room. When you enter the door, there is a wardrobe bar on one side, a toilet and shower room on the other side, a single basin washbasin outside, and a shelf under the mirror, which is very convenient for placing things. There is a balcony, but the classic and boutique hotels do not have balconies. This is very important, it is convenient for drying. I think the price of 1699 yuan for 3 days on Ctrip is worth the money. Comments should be viewed rationally. Whether it is good or not depends on whether the money is equal to the goods. Jiangxiang Technology still has work to do in the hotel business.

Check-in experience: very bad, very bad, very bad
The air conditioner is not cooling, and the air conditioner is 29-30 degrees all night. I called the switchboard and asked the engineer to go to the computer room to have a look. It was also not cooling. Fortunately, it was not hot in winter. I didn't ask the engineer to come into the room to check, but when I was about to check out at noon the next day, the air conditioner was strangely cold and dropped to 25 degrees, which was amazing.
What makes me most uncomfortable is the sound insulation of the room. Didn't the leaders of your hotel check and accept it before opening? The door gap in the room is so large that light is transmitted through, so don't you test the decibel? There are all kinds of sounds in the morning, children playing in the corridor, passersby walking, passers-by talking, dragging suitcases, room attendants knocking on other rooms' doors, the sound of dragging tool carts, and the sound of vacuum cleaners from 8 o'clock to 10 o'clock. Newly opened hotel , I was also engaged in this industry before, and I didn't want to give a bad review, because once you give a bad review, you will call me and ask me to delete it, but I really can't bear it when I saw that the price was reduced on the second day of my stay
